<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">162.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Some Power is Universal and can be used to pay for costs of any Domain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">163.</div><div class="rule-text">Basic Runes</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">163.1.</div><div class="rule-text">There are six Basic Runes , each with a Domain corresponding to its name: Fury Rune Calm Rune Mind Rune Body Rune Chaos Rune Order Rune</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">163.2.</div><div class="rule-text">A Basic Rune always has the following two Abilities :</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">163.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">[E]: [Reaction] - Add [1].</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">163.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Recycle this: [Reaction] - Add [C].</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">163.2.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The Power added this way corresponds to the Domain of the Rune that is being Recycled.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">164.</div><div class="rule-text">Rune Pools</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">165.</div><div class="rule-text">The Rune Pool is a conceptual collection of a player&#x27;s available Energy and Power available to pay Costs.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">165.1.</div><div class="rule-text">When a card adds Energy or Power, it is added to the controlling player&#x27;s Rune Pool .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">165.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Players must first add Energy and Power to their Rune Pool in order to be able to spend it to play cards or pay for Abilities with costs.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">165.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Energy and Power do not have a physical marker or tracker, although players may wish to use a physical tracker if they are retaining unspent Energy and Power over the course of their turn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">166.</div><div class="rule-text">Every player&#x27;s Rune Pool empties at the end of each player&#x27;s draw phase and the end of each player&#x27;s turn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">166.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Any unspent Energy or Power are lost.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">167.</div><div class="rule-text">All Abilities that include the action &quot; Add &quot; are abilities that are adding Energy or Power to the Rune Pool. See rule 429. Add for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">168.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">169.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields are Game Objects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">169.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields are Owned by a player.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">169.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields are not shuffled into Decks at the start of a game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">169.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields are not played during the course of regular play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">169.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields are established at the start of a game and remain in place for the duration of regular play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">169.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields cannot be Killed during the course of regular play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">169.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields cannot be Moved.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">169.5.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields are Locations.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">169.5.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields can be Origins of moves.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">169.5.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields can be Destinations of moves.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">169.6.</div><div class="rule-text">Any number of Units can be present at a Battlefield.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">169.7.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields can be targeted by spells or game effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">169.8.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields can have Passive Abilities. See rule 363. Passive Abilities for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">169.9.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields can have Triggered Abilities. See rule 382. Triggered Abilities for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">169.10.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields can be referenced in different states in card text:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">169.10.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields can be &quot;occupied.&quot; This means they have a Unit present.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">169.10.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields can be &quot;uncontrolled.&quot; This means no player controls them.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">169.10.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields can be &quot;open.&quot; This means they are unoccupied and uncontrolled.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">170.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields are not Permanents.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">171.</div><div class="rule-text">The number of Battlefields on the Board is determined by the Mode of Play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">172.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">173.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends are Game Objects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">173.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends are Owned by a player.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">173.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends are not shuffled into Decks at the start of a game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">173.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends are not played during the course of regular play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">173.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends are established at the start of a game, and remain in place for the duration of regular play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">173.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends cannot be Killed during the course of regular play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">173.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends cannot be Moved.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">173.5.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends can be targeted by spells or game effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">173.6.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends can have Passive Abilities. See rule 363. Passive Abilities for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">173.7.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends can have Triggered Abilities. See rule 382. Triggered Abilities for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">173.8.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends can have Activated Abilities. See rule 376. Activated Abilities for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">174.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends are not Permanents.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">175.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends may have one or more Domains.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">175.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The Legend determines the Domain Identity of cards its owner can include. See rule 101. Deck Construction for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">176.</div><div class="rule-text">Tokens</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">177.</div><div class="rule-text">Tokens are Game Objects created by spells and abilities during play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">178.</div><div class="rule-text">Tokens can be represented by anything. Printed tokens are included in Riftbound booster packs, but they are not required to play a token.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">179.</div><div class="rule-text">A token&#x27;s controller is the controller of the spell or ability that created it, unless the token&#x27;s type innately determines control or that spell or ability specifies that a different player is the token&#x27;s controller.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">180.</div><div class="rule-text">A token&#x27;s owner is the player who controlled the effect that created it.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">181.</div><div class="rule-text">The effect that creates a token may specify the conditions or circumstances under which it enters the board. These stipulations may alter the usual steps for playing a card.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">181.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The effect may state that the token enters ready or exhausted, if that state is contrary to the default for the token&#x27;s type.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">181.2.</div><div class="rule-text">The effect may restrict the location to which the token may be played.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">181.3.</div><div class="rule-text">The effect may grant temporary abilities or modifications to the token.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">182.</div><div class="rule-text">Tokens are not cards.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">182.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Tokens have some properties in common with cards.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">182.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Tokens are played by their owner if their card type is played, following all the applicable steps for playing a card plus any restrictions or modifications from the effect that created the token. See rule 349. Playing Cards for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">182.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Token units have a Might .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">182.1.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Tokens may have one or more tags .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">182.1.d.</div><div class="rule-text">Tokens have a type . They follow all rules for their type unless otherwise specified. Example: A token unit is a unit. It enters exhausted, can take the standard move action, deals damage equal to its Might in combat, is destroyed if it takes damage equal to or greater than its might, can be chosen or otherwise affected by spells or abilities that choose or affect units, etc.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">182.1.e.</div><div class="rule-text">Tokens inherit the recycle destination of their type. Example: Token runes will be recycled to the Rune Deck. Token units, gear, and spells will be recycled to the Main Deck. Token battlefields and legends can&#x27;t be recycled.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">182.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Tokens differ from cards in some ways.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">182.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Tokens do not have costs .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">182.2.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Although tokens do not have costs, their cost is treated as being 0 for all purposes.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">182.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Tokens do not have domains .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">183.</div><div class="rule-text">Tokens are Created on the board or the Chain and cannot exist elsewhere.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">183.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If a token is put into any Non-Board Zone besides the chain, it ceases to exist immediately after moving to its new zone.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">184.</div><div class="rule-text">The spell or ability that Creates a token specifies some of its characteristics. It may have other characteristics, as listed below.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">184.1.</div><div class="rule-text">A 1 [M] Recruit token is a domainless unit token with 1 Might and the Recruit tag.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">184.2.</div><div class="rule-text">A 3 [M] Sprite token with Temporary is a domainless unit token with 3 Might, the Fae tag, and the Temporary keyword. See rule 816. Temporary for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">184.3.</div><div class="rule-text">A 2 [M] Sand Soldier token is a domainless unit token with 2 Might and the Shurima tag.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">184.4.</div><div class="rule-text">A 3 [M] Mech token is a domainless unit token with 3 Might and the Mech tag.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">184.5.</div><div class="rule-text">A Gold gear token is a domainless gear token with &quot;[Reaction][&gt;] Kill this, [E]: [Add] [A].&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">184.6.</div><div class="rule-text">A 0 [M] Reflection token is a domainless unit token with 0 Might.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">184.7.</div><div class="rule-text">A 1 [M] Bird token is a domainless unit token with 1 Might, the Bird tag, and the Deflect keyword. See rule 809. Deflect for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">184.8.</div><div class="rule-text">A Brush battlefield token is a domainless battlefield token with &quot;Bird, Cat, Dog, Poro, and Ivern units here have +1 [M]&quot; and &quot;When you score here, you may replace this with the battlefield it replaced.&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">184.9.</div><div class="rule-text">The Baron Pit battlefield token is a domainless battlefield token with &quot;Units can move here from anywhere.&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">185.</div><div class="rule-text">Control</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">186.</div><div class="rule-text">Control is the concept of a player having influence of a Game Object and applies differently to different card types.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">187.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">187.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Control is established over Battlefields through the course of play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">187.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Control is a binary state for Battlefields and an Identifier for players.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">187.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">A Battlefield is Controlled or Uncontrolled.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">187.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">A Battlefield is Controlled by a specific player or Controlled by no one.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">187.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Control can be Contested through the course of play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">187.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Contested is a temporary status applied to the battlefield when a Unit controlled by a Player who does not currently Control that Battlefield Moves or otherwise becomes present there.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">187.3.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Units moving to or being played to a battlefield apply Contested status if that battlefield is not already contested and that Unit &#x27;s controller does not already control that battlefield.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">187.3.b.</div><div class="rule-text">A Battlefield remains Contested until Control is established or re-established.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">187.3.c.</div><div class="rule-text">The state of a Battlefield being Contested is used to determine when Combat should occur, when a Non-Combat Showdown should occur, and when Control will change.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">187.3.d.</div><div class="rule-text">At this time Game Effects cannot reference this status.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">187.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Control is established by having Units at a Battlefield at the end of a Showdown or Combat after applying the contested status.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">187.4.a.</div><div class="rule-text">If a player controls Units at a Battlefield, outside of Combat, they maintain Control of that Battlefield for as long as they have Units at that Battlefield.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">187.4.b.</div><div class="rule-text">While a Combat or Showdown is ongoing at a Battlefield , Control of that Battlefield cannot change until instructed by steps of the Combat or Showdown .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">187.4.c.</div><div class="rule-text">If a player has no Units at a Battlefield and the turn is in an Open state, they lose Control of that Battlefield in the following cleanup, unless there is a Combat or Showdown ongoing there.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">187.5.</div><div class="rule-text">Control is a constant state.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">187.6.</div><div class="rule-text">Control of a Battlefield determines Control of its Abilities.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">187.6.a.</div><div class="rule-text">While a Battlefield is Controlled , its Controller controls its Abilities . That player takes responsibility for adding them to the Chain if applicable, and makes all choices required by them unless otherwise specified.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">187.6.b.</div><div class="rule-text">While a Battlefield is Uncontrolled , its Abilities are also Uncontrolled. The Turn Player takes responsibility for adding them to the Chain if applicable, makes all choices required by them unless otherwise specified, and is treated as their Controller if any game rule or effect requires one. Example: The Arena&#x27;s Greatest is a battlefield that reads &quot;At the start of each player&#x27;s first Beginning Phase, that player gains 1 point.&quot; This ability will usually trigger while the battlefield has no controller. If it does, the Turn Player goes through the steps of adding the ability to the chain and receives priority after doing so, exactly as if they controlled the ability.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">187.6.c.</div><div class="rule-text">&quot;You&quot; in a battlefield&#x27;s abilities refers to the battlefield&#x27;s Controller , as does the implied &quot;you&quot; in instructions like &quot;draw 1.&quot; If the battlefield has no Controller , &quot;you&quot; refers to no one, and all such instructions are ignored.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">188.</div><div class="rule-text">Everything Else</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">188.1.</div><div class="rule-text">When a player Plays a Card or other Game Object , they are established as that Game Object&#x27;s Controller.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">188.2.</div><div class="rule-text">For Spells , they are the Spell&#x27;s Controller.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">188.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">That player chooses targets.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">188.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">That player chooses modes.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">188.2.c.</div><div class="rule-text">That player pays costs.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">188.3.</div><div class="rule-text">For Permanents and Runes , when they Enter the Board , that player is assigned as that Game Object&#x27;s Controller.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">188.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">That player may make decisions about the Game Object&#x27;s Inherent Abilities.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">188.3.b.</div><div class="rule-text">That player may make decisions about the Game Object&#x27;s Unique Abilities.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">188.3.c.</div><div class="rule-text">That player may make decisions about any game effects or decisions necessary while the card is being played.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">188.3.d.</div><div class="rule-text">That player may make decisions about any game effects created from &quot;When you play me&quot; effects of Permanents.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">188.4.</div><div class="rule-text">For Abilities , they are the Ability&#x27;s Controller.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">188.4.a.</div><div class="rule-text">By default, the Controller of an Ability&#x27;s Source is the Controller of that Ability.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">188.4.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Changes to Control of an Ability&#x27;s Source do not change Control of that Ability.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">188.4.c.</div><div class="rule-text">That player chooses targets.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">188.4.d.</div><div class="rule-text">That player chooses modes.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">188.4.e.</div><div class="rule-text">That player pays costs.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">189.</div><div class="rule-text">When a game effect or rules text refers to the Controller of a specific object, it can be referring to either context interchangeably.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">189.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The method of assignment of control is different, but the status of Control is the same across all Game Objects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-chapter level-0"><div class="rule-id">300.</div><div class="rule-text">Playing the Game</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">301.</div><div class="rule-text">The Turn</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">302.</div><div class="rule-text">Play continues cyclically until one player wins.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">303.</div><div class="rule-text">The phases of a turn are rigid, but the actions taken during those steps can be done in any order, unless otherwise specified.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">303.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Game Actions of any nature are performed one at a time and are executed completely.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">303.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Game Actions cannot be performed simultaneously for any reason.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">303.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">If one or more game actions, game effects, or Triggered Abilities are activated simultaneously, then Turn Order is referenced to organize the sequence of actions.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id"></div><div class="rule-text">See rule 382. Triggered Abilities for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">304.</div><div class="rule-text">The Turn Player is the player taking the current turn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">305.</div><div class="rule-text">When there are no items on the Chain and the Turn Player cannot or chooses not to perform any Discretionary Actions , the current phase or step of the turn ends and the next phase, step, or turn begins.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">306.</div><div class="rule-text">The Turn Player changes when the current Turn Player reaches the End of all of the Phases of their Turn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">307.</div><div class="rule-text">States of the Turn</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">308.</div><div class="rule-text">At any given time, the turn is in either a Neutral State or a Showdown State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">308.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If a Showdown or Combat is in progress, the turn is in a Showdown State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">308.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Only cards and abilities with the Action or Reaction keywords can be played or activated in a Showdown State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">308.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If no Showdown or Combat is in progress, the turn is in a Neutral State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">309.</div><div class="rule-text">At any given time, the turn is in either an Open State or a Closed State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">309.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If a Chain exists, the turn is in a Closed State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">309.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Only cards and abilities with the Reaction keyword can be played or activated in a Closed State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">309.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If no Chain exists, the turn is in an Open State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">310.</div><div class="rule-text">These descriptions can be combined, such that the turn is always in one of these four states:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">310.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Neutral Open: There is no Showdown or Combat in progress and no Chain exists.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">310.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">By default, cards can be played and abilities activated only when a player has priority on their turn in a Neutral Open state.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">310.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Neutral Closed: There is no Showdown or Combat in progress and a Chain exists.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">310.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Showdown Open: A Showdown or Combat is in progress and no Chain exists.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">310.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Showdown Closed: A Showdown or Combat is in progress and a Chain exists.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">311.</div><div class="rule-text">Priority and Focus</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">312.</div><div class="rule-text">At any given time, up to one player has Priority.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">312.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Priority is the singular exclusive right to take Discretionary Actions. See rule 410.1. Discretionary Actions for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">312.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The player with Priority can take appropriately timed Discretionary Actions.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">312.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">If no player has Priority , no player can take Discretionary Actions.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">312.1.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Players can always take and make choices for Limited Actions when instructed, regardless of Priority.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">312.2.</div><div class="rule-text">A player receives Priority at the following times:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">312.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">When the turn is in a Neutral Open State during their Main Phase.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">312.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">When the turn is in a Showdown State and they gain Focus.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">312.2.c.</div><div class="rule-text">When the turn is in a Closed State and they control the next item on the Chain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">312.2.d.</div><div class="rule-text">When the turn is in a Closed State , they are the next Player in Turn Order , and the player with Priority passes.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">312.3.</div><div class="rule-text">When a player is granted Priority, it is either created if no player has it or taken from the player with Priority.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">313.</div><div class="rule-text">At any given time, up to one player has Focus.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">313.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Focus is the permission to take appropriately timed Discretionary Actions when the turn is in a Showdown Open State. See rule 307. States of the Turn for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">313.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The player with Focus must obey any additional restrictions on which Discretionary Actions may be performed. Example: A player with Focus may not play spells or activate abilities that don&#x27;t have the Action or Reaction keywords.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">313.2.</div><div class="rule-text">A player who gains Focus also gains Priority.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">313.3.</div><div class="rule-text">A player who passes Priority retains Focus.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">313.4.</div><div class="rule-text">A player may not make discretionary actions with Focus unless they also possess Priority.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">313.5.</div><div class="rule-text">If the turn is in a Neutral State , no player has Focus.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">314.</div><div class="rule-text">Phases of the Turn</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">315.</div><div class="rule-text">Start of Turn</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">315.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Awaken Phase</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">315.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The following Task becomes Outstanding :</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">315.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">1. The Turn Player readies all Game Objects they control that are able to be readied. See rule 415. Ready for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">315.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Beginning Phase</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">315.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Beginning Step</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">315.2.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">At the start of Beginning Phase game effects take place.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">315.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Scoring Step</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">315.2.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The following Task becomes Outstanding :</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">315.2.b.2.</div><div class="rule-text">1. The Turn Player Holds all Battlefields they Control . See rule 462. Scoring for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">315.2.b.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Reminder: In Modes of Play with Teams , Battlefields held by a Teammate of the Turn Player during this phase are disqualified from being scored this turn by the Turn Player.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">315.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Channel Phase</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">315.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The following Task becomes Outstanding :</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">315.3.b.</div><div class="rule-text">1. The Turn Player channels 2 runes from their Rune Deck. See rule 430. Channel for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">315.3.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If there are fewer than 2 runes in the Rune Deck, they channel as many as possible.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">315.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Draw Phase</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">315.4.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The following Task becomes Outstanding :</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">315.4.b.</div><div class="rule-text">1. The Turn Player draws 1.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">315.4.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If there are no cards remaining in their Main Deck to draw, the Turn Player has been Burned Out . See rule 431. Burn Out for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">315.4.b.2.</div><div class="rule-text">After completing the Burn Out the Turn Player still Draws 1.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">315.4.c.</div><div class="rule-text">The following Task becomes Outstanding:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">315.4.d.</div><div class="rule-text">1. Each player&#x27;s Rune Pool empties. Any unspent Energy and Power are lost. See rule 164. Rune Pools for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">316.</div><div class="rule-text">Main Phase</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">316.1.</div><div class="rule-text">When all steps of the Start of Turn have been completed, the Main Phase begins.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">316.2.</div><div class="rule-text">The Main Phase has no defined structure.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">316.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">A player may take any number of Discretionary Actions they are able to perform during this phase. See rule 410.1. Discretionary Actions for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">316.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">This is denoted as a Neutral Open State , and only the Turn Player has the ability to play spells or activate abilities. See rule 307. States of the Turn for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">316.2.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">In Modes of Play with teammates, the Turn Player&#x27;s teammates may play spells and activate abilities, including ones without Action or Reaction. They can only do so when the Turn Player invites them to do so with their own Priority.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">316.3.</div><div class="rule-text">As a result of a player taking Discretionary Actions , one or more structured phases may occur.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">316.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Combat</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">316.4.a.</div><div class="rule-text">A Combat occurs as a result of Units controlled by opposing players being present at the same Battlefield .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">316.4.b.</div><div class="rule-text">This could be the result of a Standard Move Standard Action , a Spell , or other Game Effect.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">316.4.c.</div><div class="rule-text">The source effect does not change the structure or flow of Combat once initiated.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">316.4.d.</div><div class="rule-text">A Combat can only occur between two players. See rule 454. Combat for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">316.4.e.</div><div class="rule-text">Play proceeds following the steps of combat. See rule 458. The Steps of Combat for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">316.4.f.</div><div class="rule-text">Combat will also include a Showdown.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">316.5.</div><div class="rule-text">Showdowns</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">316.5.a.</div><div class="rule-text">A Showdown occurs when a Combat occurs.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">316.5.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Showdowns that occur as a result of Combat are a Sub-Phase of Combat.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">316.5.b.</div><div class="rule-text">A Showdown is marked as Staged at a Battlefield when the Contested status is applied to a Battlefield with no current controller.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">316.5.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Showdowns that occur as a result of a player moving to an empty Battlefield are a stand-alone Phase and do not create a Combat.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-4"><div class="rule-id">316.5.b.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">These Showdowns are called Non-Combat Showdowns . During the proceedings of a Non-Combat Showdown , units controlled by a different player may become present at the Battlefield where the Showdown is ongoing. This will cause the Showdown to become a Combat Showdown.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">316.5.c.</div><div class="rule-text">A Showdown is a structured Window of Opportunity where Players may play cards and activate abilities with Action or Reaction. See rule 341. Showdowns for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">316.6.</div><div class="rule-text">When a player has no more Discretionary Actions they wish to execute, they must indicate they are ending their turn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">316.6.a.</div><div class="rule-text">This ends the Main Phase.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">316.6.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Play proceeds to the Ending Phase.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">317.</div><div class="rule-text">Ending Phase</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">317.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Ending Step</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">317.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">At the end of the turn Game Effects take place.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">317.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Specific game effects and abilities will reference this timing and phase as necessary.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">317.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Expiration Step</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">317.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Invoke an Ending Special Cleanup. See rule 318. Cleanups for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">317.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Insert &quot;2c. Heal all Units .&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">317.2.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Insert &quot;2d. All &#x27;this turn&#x27; effects expire simultaneously.&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">317.2.d.</div><div class="rule-text">Insert &quot;2e. Each player&#x27;s Rune Pool empties. Any unspent Energy and Power are lost.&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">317.2.e.</div><div class="rule-text">The following Task becomes Outstanding :</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">317.2.f.</div><div class="rule-text">1. If any items underwent the FEPR process, return to the start of the Expiration Step</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">317.3.</div><div class="rule-text">The next player with their Turn queued becomes the Turn Player.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">318.</div><div class="rule-text">Cleanups</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">319.</div><div class="rule-text">A Cleanup will be made an Outstanding Task at the following times:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">319.1.</div><div class="rule-text">After the game transitions to or from an Open or Closed state</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">319.2.</div><div class="rule-text">After the game transitions between Phases, unless specified otherwise</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">319.3.</div><div class="rule-text">After a Pending Item is added to the Chain</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">319.4.</div><div class="rule-text">After a Pending Item becomes a Legal Item on the Chain</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">319.5.</div><div class="rule-text">After a Chain Item is removed from the Chain for any reason</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">319.6.</div><div class="rule-text">After any number of Game Objects enter or leave the Board</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">319.7.</div><div class="rule-text">After the status of any number of Game Objects changes for any reason</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">319.8.</div><div class="rule-text">After a Move is completed</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">320.</div><div class="rule-text">While a Cleanup is occurring, Chain Items cannot be Resolved.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">320.1.</div><div class="rule-text">New Pending Items can be added, but Legal Items cannot be executed and Priority and Focus are not passed or awarded.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">321.</div><div class="rule-text">Similarly, while Chain Items are Resolving , a Cleanup cannot occur.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">321.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If an event occurs during the Resolution of a Chain Item that qualifies for a Cleanup , that Cleanup will be made an Outstanding Task.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">322.</div><div class="rule-text">If an event occurs during a Cleanup that qualifies for a Cleanup, another Cleanup will occur immediately after the first completes, repeating until a Cleanup occurs with no new change in the game&#x27;s state.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">322.1.</div><div class="rule-text">These new Cleanups are themselves Outstanding Tasks.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">323.</div><div class="rule-text">When a Cleanup occurs, the following Tasks become Outstanding in the order described:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">323.1.</div><div class="rule-text">1. If a player has points greater than or equal to the Victory Score, and more points than any opponent, that player wins.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">323.2.</div><div class="rule-text">2. Assign or Remove the Attacker or Defender designation from Units as needed if there is a Combat in progress</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">323.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">If there are Units present at the Battlefield the Combat is taking place at, but do not have a designation, they gain the same designation as their Controller now</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">323.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">If there are Units present at the Battlefield the Combat is taking place at, but have the opposite designation of their controller, they lose that designation, and gain the same designation as their controller now</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">323.2.c.</div><div class="rule-text">If there are Units at locations other than the Battlefield that the Combat is taking place at, but have either Attacker or Defender designations, they lose those designations now</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">323.3.</div><div class="rule-text">3. Handle outstanding board state</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">323.4.</div><div class="rule-text">3a. All Units that have non-zero Damage marked on them equalling or exceeding their Might that have Deathknell abilities will trigger their Deathknell ability now, making note of their current location, attributes, and other information relevant to add the trigger as a Pending Item See rule 808 Deathknell for more information .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">323.5.</div><div class="rule-text">3b. All Units that have non-zero Damage marked on them equalling or exceeding their Might are killed and placed in their owners&#x27; Trash.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">323.6.</div><div class="rule-text">4. If the turn is in an Open State, Battlefields with no Units occupying them and no Showdown or Combat ongoing become Uncontrolled.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">323.7.</div><div class="rule-text">5. Recall all Unattached non- Unit Gear at Battlefields, and all Permanents and Runes in Bases other than their controller&#x27;s. Remove all Hidden cards from all Battlefields that are not controlled by the same player and place them in their owner&#x27;s Trash.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">323.8.</div><div class="rule-text">6. Mark a Showdown as Staged at each Battlefield that Contested was applied to.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">323.8.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The Showdown remains Staged at each Battlefield that is Contested and has units present controlled by the player that applied Contested.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">323.9.</div><div class="rule-text">7. Mark a Combat as Staged at each Battlefield that Contested was applied to that have Units present controlled by opposing players.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">323.9.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The Combat remains Staged at that Battlefield as long as there are Units present from two opposing players there.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">323.10.</div><div class="rule-text">7a. If Units of two opposing players are no longer present at a Battlefield that has a Combat Staged before it has opened, the Combat will cease being Staged</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">323.11.</div><div class="rule-text">8. If the current state is a Neutral Open State and one or more Showdowns are Staged , the Turn Player chooses one of those Battlefields. A Showdown begins there.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">323.12.</div><div class="rule-text">8a. If a Showdown and Combat are staged at the same Battlefield and the turn player chooses to initiate the Showdown there, the Showdown will open as a Combat Showdown.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">323.13.</div><div class="rule-text">9. If the current state is a Neutral Open State and Combat is Staged at one or more Battlefields , the Turn Player chooses one of those Battlefields . Combat begins there.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">323.14.</div><div class="rule-text">9a. If the current state is Showdown Open State and Combat is Staged at a Battlefield where there is a Non-Combat Showdown ongoing, that Showdown becomes a Combat Showdown.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">324.</div><div class="rule-text">Special Cleanups are Cleanup steps invoked at specific times that have additional steps not present in a normal Cleanup.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">324.1.</div><div class="rule-text">When a Special Cleanup is invoked, the unique steps added will be inserted and defined by the sub-section that invokes it. Example: When a Combat Cleanup is invoked, the Combat section defines what steps are added to the Cleanup. See rule 461. The Resolution Step for more information. Example: When an End of Turn Cleanup is invoked, the End of Turn Phase subsection defines what steps are added to the Cleanup. See rule 317. The Ending Phase for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">324.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If events during a Special Cleanup require another Cleanup, a normal Cleanup is invoked, not another iteration of the Special Cleanup .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">325.</div><div class="rule-text">Chains and Showdowns</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">326.</div><div class="rule-text">Players can act during the following Windows of Opportunity that occur during the course of regular play:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">326.1.</div><div class="rule-text">During a Chain</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">326.2.</div><div class="rule-text">During a Showdown</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">327.</div><div class="rule-text">Chains</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">328.</div><div class="rule-text">The Chain is a Non-Board Zone that temporarily exists whenever a card is played or an ability is activated.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">328.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Cards are placed here as part of the process of being played.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">328.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Abilities are queued here as part of the process of resolving. See rule 360. Abilities for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">329.</div><div class="rule-text">Cards and abilities added to the chain are added as Pending Chain Items that become Finalized Chain Items.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">329.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Pending Items are on the Chain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">329.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Chain Items are Pending until the &quot;Check Legality&quot; step of playing a card. See rule 349. Playing Cards for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">329.3.</div><div class="rule-text">When a Pending Chain Item is no longer Pending it is finalized and becomes a Finalized Chain Item .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">330.</div><div class="rule-text">The Chain exists as long as a Chain Item is on it.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">330.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Only one Chain can exist at a time.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">330.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If a card would begin to be played while a Chain already exists, it is placed on the existing Chain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">331.</div><div class="rule-text">The State of the Turn is partially determined by whether or not the Chain currently exists.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">331.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The turn is said to be in a Closed State if a Chain exists.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">331.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Cards of all Categories, by default, cannot be played during a Closed State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">331.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Card abilities, by default, cannot be played during a Closed State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">331.2.</div><div class="rule-text">The turn is said to be in an Open State if no Chain exists.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">332.</div><div class="rule-text">Steps of Resolving Chain Items</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">333.</div><div class="rule-text">Whenever a card or token is played or an ability is activated or triggered, a Chain is created.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">333.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The player that created the chain becomes the first player with Priority.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">334.</div><div class="rule-text">A Task is one or more steps or processes that one or more Players must perform before continuing with any other actions.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">334.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Tasks include, but are not limited to: Cleanups , the actions performed during the Start of Turn Process , throughout Combat in its various steps, and the actions performed during the End of Turn Process. See rule 318. Cleanups for more information on Cleanups See rule 315. Start of Turn for more information on the Start of Turn process See rule 454. Combat for more information on the steps of Combat See rule 317. Ending Phase for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">335.</div><div class="rule-text">Whenever a Player takes one or more actions that incur Tasks they should refer to the process of HOT FEPR: H andle O utstanding T asks; then F inalize, E xecute, P ass, R esolve.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">335.1.</div><div class="rule-text">In the course of Handling Outstanding Tasks, Chain Items may be added to the Chain . They will remain there until the Tasks are complete.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">335.2.</div><div class="rule-text">When all Outstanding Tasks are completed, all pending Chain Items will subsequently be processed by the FEPR process.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">335.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">During the FEPR process, new Tasks may be incurred. Pause the process and complete the necessary Tasks before continuing.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">335.3.</div><div class="rule-text">If there are no Outstanding Tasks , no pending Chain Items , and it is the Main Phase, the Turn Player receives priority. If there are no Outstanding Tasks , no pending items, and it is any other phase of the turn, proceed to the next substep, step, phase, or turn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">336.</div><div class="rule-text">When there are no outstanding Tasks and there are pending Chain Items on the Chain , players should refer to the FEPR process to proceed.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">336.1.</div><div class="rule-text">In the sequence of resolving FEPR more Chain Items may become Pending Chain Items . These will be processed by the same FEPR process that produced them.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">337.</div><div class="rule-text">Step 1: Finalize</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">337.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If one or more Items are Pending , their controllers must complete the steps of Playing those Pending Items until they are Finalized Items or leave the Chain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">337.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">This process does not pass Priority.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">337.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Each Item is Finalized in the order it was appended to the Chain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">337.1.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Units, Gear, and abilities that Add resources resolve immediately when Finalized and do not progress to Step 2: Execute. See rule 349. Playing Cards for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">337.1.c.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If the Chain is empty, play proceeds in an Open State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-4"><div class="rule-id">337.1.c.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">If this occurs during a Showdown , the next player in turn order gains Focus .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">337.1.c.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If the Chain is not empty and there are one or more Pending Items , repeat Step 1.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">337.1.c.3.</div><div class="rule-text">If the Chain is not empty and there are no Pending Items , the controller of the newest item on the chain gains Priority and becomes the Active Player. Proceed to Step 2: Execute.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">338.</div><div class="rule-text">Step 2: Execute</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">338.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The player with Priority may do any the following:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">338.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Play a Card that is legally timed.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">338.1.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Cards , by default, cannot be played during a Closed State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">338.1.a.2.</div><div class="rule-text">A Legally Timed Card would be a Card with Reaction or a card that will have Reaction when played under appropriate circumstances.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">338.1.a.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Other exceptions may be created during regular play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">338.1.a.4.</div><div class="rule-text">The card will be added to the chain as a Pending Item , following the steps of playing a card.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">338.1.a.5.</div><div class="rule-text">This can be an additional card to the item that Started the Chain in the case of the first player with Priority after creating the Chain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">338.1.a.6.</div><div class="rule-text">Whether a Card is legally timed is evaluated during the &quot;Check Legality&quot; step of Playing a Card. See rule 349. Playing Cards for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">338.1.a.7.</div><div class="rule-text">Playing a card will create one or more Pending Items . Return to Step 1: Finalize.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">338.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Activate Abilities of Game Objects that are legally timed. See rule 398. Playing or Activating Abilities for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">338.1.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">All rules for legally timed cards apply to legally timed abilities.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">338.1.b.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Activating abilities will create one or more Pending Items . Return to Step 1: Finalize.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">338.1.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Pass Priority</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">338.1.c.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The player with Priority passes Priority to the next Player in Turn Order. Proceed to Step 3: Pass.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">339.</div><div class="rule-text">Step 3: Pass</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">339.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If all players have passed Priority without adding any items to the Chain , proceed to Step 4: Resolve.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">339.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Otherwise, the player with Priority passes Priority to the next Player in Turn Order. Return to Step 3: Execute.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">340.</div><div class="rule-text">Step 4: Resolve</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">340.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The newest item on the Chain resolves. Execute its game effects in their entirety. See rule 349. Playing Cards for more information on resolving spells. See rule 398. Playing or Activating Abilities for more information on resolving abilities.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">340.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If the Chain is empty, play proceeds in an Open State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">340.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">If this occurs during a Showdown , focus passes to the next player in turn order.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">340.3.</div><div class="rule-text">If the Chain is not empty and there are one or more Pending Items , return to Step 1: Finalize.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">340.4.</div><div class="rule-text">If the Chain is not empty and there are no Pending Items , the controller of the newest item on the chain gains Priority . Return to Step 2: Execute.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">341.</div><div class="rule-text">Showdowns</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">342.</div><div class="rule-text">A Showdown is a Window of Opportunity in which Players have an Open State in which they may play Spells in an alternating fashion.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">342.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Each spell played this way creates a Chain as normal.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">343.</div><div class="rule-text">The State of the turn is partially determined by whether or not a Showdown or Combat is in progress.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">343.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The turn is said to be in a Showdown State if a Showdown or Combat is in progress.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">343.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Cards of all Categories, by default, cannot be played during a Showdown State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">343.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Card abilities, by default, cannot be played during a Showdown State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">343.2.</div><div class="rule-text">The turn is said to be in a Neutral State if no Showdown or Combat is in progress.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">344.</div><div class="rule-text">A Showdown begins when Control of a Battlefield is Contested and the turn is in a Neutral Open State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">344.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If Control of a Battlefield is Contested between two players, then a Showdown will be opened as the first step of Combat. See rule 454. Combat for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">344.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If Control of a Battlefield is Contested and the Battlefield in question is uncontrolled when it becomes Contested , a Showdown is opened during the Cleanup at the end of the action that caused the Battlefield to become Contested.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">345.</div><div class="rule-text">As a Showdown begins, the player who applied Contested status to the Battlefield gains Focus.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">346.</div><div class="rule-text">When the last item on the chain resolves and the turn returns to an Open State during a Showdown , Focus passes, and the next Player gains both Focus and Priority.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">346.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Focus will not pass in this way if the chain opened as a result of a triggered ability being added to the chain, nor if it opened as a result of an Add ability being added to the chain. Example: the Initial Chain opens as a result of triggered abilities being added to the chain, so when the last item on the Initial Chain resolves and the turn returns to an Open State, Focus will not pass.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">347.</div><div class="rule-text">During a Showdown , the player with Focus may do one of the following:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">347.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Play a card that is legally timed.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">347.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The card will start a Chain as normal.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">347.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Activate Abilities of Game Objects that are legally timed. See rule 360. Abilities for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">347.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Pass.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">347.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">If all Players have passed once in sequence, the Showdown ends.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">347.3.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Perform a Cleanup.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">347.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Otherwise, Focus passes to the next Player in Turn Order.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">348.</div><div class="rule-text">If all players pass Focus without playing a spell or activating an ability, then the Showdown Closes.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">348.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If it is a Combat Showdown, proceed with the remaining steps of Combat to resolve the phase. See rule 458. The Steps of Combat for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">348.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If it is a Non-Combat Showdown, do the following:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">348.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">If only one player&#x27;s Units remain at the Battlefield , and if that player does not already Control the Battlefield , that player establishes Control over the Battlefield . See rule 185. Control for more information on Control . See rule 464.1. for more information on Conquering .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">348.2.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">This results in a Conquer if that player has not yet scored that Battlefield this turn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">349.</div><div class="rule-text">Playing Cards</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">350.</div><div class="rule-text">Playing a card is the act of a player utilizing their cards.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">350.1.</div><div class="rule-text">A card is Played when it has finished this process in its entirety.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">350.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Tokens are not cards, but can still be Played. See rule 176. Tokens for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">351.</div><div class="rule-text">Cards have different behaviors when played.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">351.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Permanents become Game Objects when Played.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">351.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Spells create game effects that are executed, then the card is placed in the trash when Played.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">352.</div><div class="rule-text">Cards have different states during the process of being played.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">352.1.</div><div class="rule-text">When initially being played cards are Pending, as Pending Chain Items.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">352.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Near the end of the process cards will cease being Pending and become Finalized Chain Items .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">353.</div><div class="rule-text">The Process of Play</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">354.</div><div class="rule-text">1. Remove the card from the zone you are playing it from and put it onto the Chain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">354.1.</div><div class="rule-text">This Closes the State. See rule 307. States of the Turn for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">354.2.</div><div class="rule-text">This item becomes Pending, awaiting the finalization process (steps 2 - 5)</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">354.3.</div><div class="rule-text">If another Card Effect or ability is currently resolving, continue resolving it before proceeding with any further steps of this process.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">354.4.</div><div class="rule-text">If there are Tasks outstanding or currently being handled, finish those Tasks before continuing this process. See rule 334. for more information on Tasks.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">355.</div><div class="rule-text">2. Make relevant choices.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">355.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If the card is a spell, or has an effect that specifies a choice &quot;As I am played,&quot; those choices are made now.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">355.2.</div><div class="rule-text">For Units , choose a valid Location where that Unit will be placed upon being Played.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">355.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">By default, Valid locations include the controller&#x27;s Base or a Battlefield the controller controls.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">355.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Some Game Effects may grant players permission to play Units to locations that are not normally Valid . Such locations become Valid for the purposes of Playing the Unit.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">355.3.</div><div class="rule-text">For Spells and Abilities with a bulleted list of modes to choose from, make the appropriate choices now.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">355.4.</div><div class="rule-text">For Spells and Abilities that Move one or more Units , choose a valid Location as the Move Destination for each Move that will be performed.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">355.4.a.</div><div class="rule-text">A valid Location is one other than the Units&#x27; current Location where they are allowed to be present.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">355.5.</div><div class="rule-text">If a card requires you to specifically choose one or more Game Objects , that choice is made now.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">355.5.a.</div><div class="rule-text">This does not include cards that affect one or more Game Objects based on criteria. Example: &quot;Stun a unit at a battlefield&quot; is a Choice. Example: &quot;Kill all gear&quot; is not a Choice.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">355.5.b.</div><div class="rule-text">This does not include making choices for Triggered Abilities of permanents, even if those abilities trigger when the permanent is played. Example: A unit with a triggered ability that says &quot;When I&#x27;m played, kill a unit&quot; does not require you to choose a target as it&#x27;s played. The target will be chosen when the ability triggers. See rule 382. Triggered Abilities for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">355.6.</div><div class="rule-text">Targeting</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">355.7.</div><div class="rule-text">When a card Chooses one or more specific Game Objects to affect, it is Targeted unless indicated otherwise by the rules in this section.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">355.8.</div><div class="rule-text">In order to put a spell or ability on the chain, valid choices must be made for all targets.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">355.9.</div><div class="rule-text">A target is a valid choice if it meets all of the following requirements:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">355.9.a.</div><div class="rule-text">It is a permanent or rune on the board, a spell or ability on the chain, a player or zone, or specified explicitly or implicitly as being in some other zone. e.g., &quot;Kill a unit&quot; targets a unit on the board. e.g., &quot;Recycle a unit from your trash&quot; targets a unit card in your trash.</div></div>
