<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">438.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Replacing is the act of Creating a token in the place of another card or token without playing it while inheriting all effects or statuses of the game object it replaced.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">438.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Replacing is a Limited Action.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">438.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The player may Replace cards and tokens when instructed to do so by other game effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">438.3.</div><div class="rule-text">This action, when instructed, is formatted as &quot;Replace [X] with [Y].&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">438.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The [X] is the target to be Replaced.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">438.3.b.</div><div class="rule-text">The [Y] is the object that will Replace the target.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">438.3.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">This will always specify a Token to create.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">438.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Replacing is not a subset of Banishing.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">438.5.</div><div class="rule-text">The card or token that is Replaced is placed in Banishment.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">438.5.a.</div><div class="rule-text">While it resides in Banishment, it is considered to have been Replaced and not Banished.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">438.6.</div><div class="rule-text">If a token is Replaced it will stop existing once it begins its occupancy in Banishment.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">438.6.a.</div><div class="rule-text">This does not invalidate the token created, or the act of Replacement.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">438.7.</div><div class="rule-text">Tokens that have been Created through a Replace action can be instructed to be &quot;Swapped back.&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">438.7.a.</div><div class="rule-text">&quot;Swapping Back&quot; is an extension of the Replace action.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">438.7.b.</div><div class="rule-text">To Swap Back , the token stops existing and the original card is returned to the space that the token just occupied, inheriting all current effects and statuses.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">438.7.c.</div><div class="rule-text">If there is nothing in Banishment to swap back to, usually because a token was replaced, then this object can never swap back.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">439.</div><div class="rule-text">Create</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">439.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Creating is the act of producing a Game Object that previously did not exist in the game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">439.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Effects that Create one or more Game Objects will direct where those Game Objects must go - the Game Objects are Created directly to the zones in question.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">439.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Prior to being Created, these Game Objects did not exist outside of the zone they were Created to. After being Created , they may change zones as appropriate for Game Objects of their type.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">439.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">If a zone is not specified by the effect, the Game Object will be created to the appropriate zone for its type.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-cont level-1"><div class="rule-id"></div><div class="rule-text">Permanents will be Created to any location on the Board that they can be played to.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">439.2.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Spells will be Created to the Chain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">439.2.b.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Runes will be Created to base.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">439.2.b.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends will be Created to the Legend Zone.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">439.2.b.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields will be Created to the Battlefield Zone.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">439.3.</div><div class="rule-text">An effect that Creates a Game Object will specify the nature of the Game Object created.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">439.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">If the Game Object is a token, it will follow the normal rules for tokens. See rule 176. Tokens for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">439.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Unless specified otherwise by the Game Effect that Creates a Game Object , any such Game Object is owned by the player who Created it. Control is established as usual for Game Objects of the</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-cont level-1"><div class="rule-id"></div><div class="rule-text">appropriate</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id"></div><div class="rule-text">type.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">439.4.a.</div><div class="rule-text">A Created permanent, rune, legend, or spell is controlled by its owner as it is created.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">439.4.b.</div><div class="rule-text">A Created battlefield is uncontrolled as it is created.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">439.5.</div><div class="rule-text">This action, when instructed, is usually formatted as &quot;Create [X] to [Y]&quot; or &quot;Add [X] to [Y].&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">439.6.</div><div class="rule-text">Creating is a Limited Action.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">439.6.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Players may only Create Game Objects when directed to by Game Effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">440.</div><div class="rule-text">Movement</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">441.</div><div class="rule-text">Moving is a Limited Action.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">441.1.</div><div class="rule-text">A Permanent changing its position from any space on the Board to another space on the Board is a Move , unless it is caused by a corrective Recall . See rule 420. Move for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">441.2.</div><div class="rule-text">A card changing game zones does not in itself constitute a Move.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">441.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Moving is instantaneous.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">441.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">There is no state for Permanents between locations.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">441.3.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Permanents are either at their Origin before Moving or their Destination after Moving.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">441.3.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Moving does not use the Chain , nor is it able to be Reacted to.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">442.</div><div class="rule-text">Moving is defined by the Origin and Destination of the Permanent that is changing locations.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">442.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The Origin is where the Permanent is starting from.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">442.2.</div><div class="rule-text">The Destination is where the Permanent is going to.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">442.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">In Modes of Play with more than two players, Battlefields with Staged Combats or Combats in Progress are Invalid Destinations for Moves of all kinds ( Standard Moves or otherwise) by Units controlled by Players not involved in those Combats or who don&#x27;t already have permanents at that Battlefield .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">442.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">In Modes of Play with teammates, Battlefields Controlled by a player&#x27;s teammates are Invalid Destinations for Moves of all kinds ( Standard Moves or otherwise) by Units that player controls.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">442.2.c.</div><div class="rule-text">If an action would require a Move that would cause a Unit to become present in a Location where it cannot move for any reason, such as a Battlefield with two players that are not the controller of the Unit performing this Move action are in a Combat or such a Combat is Staged , it instead Recalls. See rule 449. Recalls for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">442.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Units are the only Permanents that can Move.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">443.</div><div class="rule-text">Players may choose to move their Units with the Standard Move. See rule 144. for more information on the Standard Move.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">444.</div><div class="rule-text">Spells , Abilities , or other effects may cause a Move to occur.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">444.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The source of the Move will provide details on any restrictions on legality for Destination.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">444.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Units cannot Move to a Battlefield that already has units from 2 other players present by any means.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">445.</div><div class="rule-text">The Destination becomes Contested if it is a Battlefield not controlled by the controller of the Unit or Units that moved.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">446.</div><div class="rule-text">Units may cause a Showdown without a Combat when they Move.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">446.1.</div><div class="rule-text">A Showdown is opened when a Move causes a Battlefield to become Contested while it has no Units present from any player other than those that just moved.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">447.</div><div class="rule-text">Units may cause Combat when they Move.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">447.1.</div><div class="rule-text">A Combat is opened when a Move causes a Battlefield to become Contested and Units controlled by opposing players, or when a Move causes Units controlled by opposing players to become present in the same Battlefield where a Showdown is ongoing. See rule 454. Combat for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">448.</div><div class="rule-text">When a Move action is complete, perform a Cleanup.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">449.</div><div class="rule-text">Recalls</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">450.</div><div class="rule-text">A Recall is when a Permanent is relocated from anywhere to its Base without it being a Move.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">451.</div><div class="rule-text">Recalls are not Moves.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">451.1.</div><div class="rule-text">They do not cause Triggered Abilities to trigger that are triggered by Move actions.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">451.2.</div><div class="rule-text">A Recall causes a Permanent to change locations.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">451.3.</div><div class="rule-text">A Recall cannot be prevented by actions and Game Effects that restrict or block Movement.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">452.</div><div class="rule-text">Gear can be Recalled.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">452.1.</div><div class="rule-text">When an un-attached Gear is created or played at a battlefield, or is at a battlefield for any other reason, it is Recalled to its controller&#x27;s base during the next Cleanup. Example: An Equipment is attached to a unit at a battlefield, so the Equipment is present at that battlefield. If the unit dies, the Equipment will be recalled during the next cleanup.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">453.</div><div class="rule-text">Recalls do not affect the state of the Permanent being recalled.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">453.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Unless otherwise stated by the source of the Recall , Damage, Exhausted Status, Buffed Status, and applied Layer alterations will all remain unaffected by a Recall .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">454.</div><div class="rule-text">Combat</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">455.</div><div class="rule-text">A Combat occurs when a Cleanup occurs, there are no items on the Chain , there is a staged Combat at a Battlefield, and no Showdown or Combat is ongoing at any other Battlefield. See rule 318. Cleanups for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">455.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If there is an ongoing Showdown at the Battlefield where the Combat is staged, that Showdown will become a Combat Showdown and a Combat will be initiated there.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">456.</div><div class="rule-text">Combat is considered Staged if there are units controlled by two opposing players at a Battlefield but the Steps of Combat have not been initiated.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">456.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If more than one Battlefield has Units controlled by opposing players at it at the same time, the Turn Player decides which Combat to resolve first.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">456.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If Staged Combats stop being Staged before the Steps of Combat are initiated, they are not resolved or executed.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">456.3.</div><div class="rule-text">If a Combat and Showdown are staged at the same Battlefield and the turn player initiates the</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id"></div><div class="rule-text">Showdown , it will open as a Combat Showdown.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">457.</div><div class="rule-text">Combat can only occur between Units controlled by exactly two players.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">457.1.</div><div class="rule-text">In Modes of Play with more than two players, Battlefields with Staged Combats or Combats in Progress are Invalid Destinations for Moves of all kinds ( Standard Moves or otherwise) by Units controlled by Players not involved in those Combats or who don&#x27;t already have Units at that Battlefield. See rule 442.2.a. for more information on Invalid Destinations.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">457.2.</div><div class="rule-text">In Modes of Play with more than two players, Battlefields with Staged Combats or Combats in Progress are Invalid to be chosen as a location to play one or more Units by a player not involved in that Combat by any means,</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">457.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">If an effect would require a Unit be played to a Battlefield with a Staged Combat or a Combat in Progress , where the controller of the played unit is not a participant, instead the Unit is played to its controller&#x27;s Base.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">457.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Any subsequent reference to &quot;here&quot; in the corresponding effect is reassigned to the Controller&#x27;s Base , where the Unit was played. Any further effects that may be invalidated are invalidated as if the effect was mistargeted. See rule 355.6. Targeting for more information on Mistargeting.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">457.3.</div><div class="rule-text">All choices that would result in a Combat occurring between more than two players simultaneously are invalid and ineligible to be completed.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">458.</div><div class="rule-text">The Steps of Combat</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">459.</div><div class="rule-text">Step 1: The Combat Showdown Step</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">459.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Combat will open in one of two ways: when a Combat and Showdown are staged at the same Battlefield and the turn player initiates the Showdown ; or when the turn is in a Showdown Open State and a Combat is staged at the Battlefield where the current Showdown is ongoing. See rule 318. Cleanups for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">459.2.</div><div class="rule-text">When Combat opens, it either opens with a Combat Showdown, or the current Showdown becomes a Combat Showdown.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">459.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The following Tasks become Outstanding , in the order described:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">459.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">1. Establish who is Attacker and who is Defender.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">459.2.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The Attacker is the player whose unit(s) applied the Contested status to the Battlefield. They gain the Attacker designation now.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-4"><div class="rule-id">459.2.b.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">This player gains Focus as the showdown begins.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">459.2.b.2.</div><div class="rule-text">The Defender is the player who did not apply the Contested status to the Battlefield. They gain the Defender designation now.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">459.2.b.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Units at the Contested Battlefield controlled by the Attacker gain the Attacker designation now.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-4"><div class="rule-id">459.2.b.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">If a Unit controlled by the Attacker becomes present at this Battlefield after this moment, it will gain the Attacker designation during the Cleanup phase following the action that caused it to become present</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">459.2.b.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Units at the Contested Battlefield controlled by the Defender gain the Defender designation now.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-4"><div class="rule-id">459.2.b.4.a.</div><div class="rule-text">If a Unit controlled by the Defender becomes present at this Battlefield after this moment it will gain the Defender designation during the Cleanup phase following the action that caused it to become present</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">459.2.c.</div><div class="rule-text">2. The Attacker gains Focus.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">459.2.d.</div><div class="rule-text">3. Add items to the Combat Chain if establishing Attacker and Defender has caused Triggered Abilities to become Pending.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">459.2.d.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The Attacking player, who has Focus , places Triggered Abilities on the Chain first, followed by all non- Defender players in Turn Order , followed by the Defending Player.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">459.2.e.</div><div class="rule-text">The State Closes if a Combat Chain was created.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">459.2.e.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Otherwise the Combat Showdown continues, with the State Open as normal.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">459.2.f.</div><div class="rule-text">Players proceed with any play on the Chain as normal.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">459.2.g.</div><div class="rule-text">Focus does not pass upon closure of the Combat Chain, if any.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">460.</div><div class="rule-text">Step 2: The Combat Damage Step</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">460.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If both Attacking and Defending units remain at this battlefield, the following Tasks become Outstanding , in the specified order:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">460.2.</div><div class="rule-text">1. When the Showdown closes, Attackers and Defenders resolve Combat Damage at the Battlefield that was attacked, using their current Might.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">460.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Sum the Might of all Attacking Units.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">460.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Sum the Might of all Defending Units.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">460.2.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Starting with the Attacker , each player assigns an amount of damage equal to their summed Might among the other&#x27;s Units.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">460.2.c.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Assigning Damage is not Dealing Damage.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-4"><div class="rule-id">460.2.c.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">When all Damage is assigned, it will be Dealt simultaneously. These actions are not synonymous.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">460.2.c.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Abilities or effects may influence the order in which damage is assigned. Reminder: Lethal Damage is non-zero damage equaling or exceeding the Might of a Unit.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">460.2.c.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Units must have lethal damage assigned to them in full before damage is assigned to a different Unit. Example: If a player has 5 damage to distribute among four 3 Might units, they may not choose to assign 2 damage to one of the units and 1 damage to each of the remaining 3. They must assign at least 3 damage to one, and the remaining 2 to another.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">460.2.c.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Units cannot have more damage assigned to them than the minimum required to constitute lethal damage unless no further units remain to have damage assigned to them.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">460.2.c.5.</div><div class="rule-text">A player must obey all requirements and restrictions on damage assignment if able. Example: A player is assigning damage to the following units: a unit with Tank (&quot;I must be assigned combat damage first.&quot;); Caitlyn, Patrolling (&quot;I must be assigned combat damage last.&quot;); and another unit without any abilities. That player must assign combat damage first to the unit with Tank, then to the unit with no abilities, then to Caitlyn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">460.2.c.6.</div><div class="rule-text">If multiple Units have abilities or effects that require a player to assign them damage with the same priority, that player may assign damage to those units in any order. Example: A player is assigning damage to the following units: two units with Tank (&quot;I must be assigned combat damage first.&quot;) and one unit with no abilities. That player chooses one of the units with Tank and assigns combat damage to it. Then they must assign any remaining damage first to the other unit with Tank, then to the unit with no abilities.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">460.2.c.7.</div><div class="rule-text">If a Unit has one or more Abilities or effects applying to it that demand it be assigned damage in a specific way that is exclusionary, then the assigning player chooses only one of those abilities to apply when assigning damage. Example: Caitlyn, Patrolling (&quot;I must be assigned combat damage last.&quot;) has been given the Tank ability (&quot;I must be assigned combat damage first.&quot;). A player is assigning damage to this Caitlyn with Tank and two units with no abilities. That player can&#x27;t fulfill both of Caitlyn&#x27;s damage requirements, so they may choose to assign damage to Caitlyn first, fulfilling the Tank requirement, or last, fulfilling Caitlyn&#x27;s printed requirement. They can&#x27;t choose to apply damage to Caitlyn in between the other two units, because that wouldn&#x27;t fulfill either requirement.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">460.2.c.8.</div><div class="rule-text">If there is more than one unit in which this situation applies to, each unit is dealt with individually. The assigning player chooses which ability or effect applies, and then resolves the assignment. If this creates a situation where now more than one unit must be assigned with the same priority, those units may be assigned damage in any order as normal within that priority. Example: Two copies of Caitlyn, Patrolling (&quot;I must be assigned combat damage last.&quot;) have been given the Tank ability (&quot;I must be assigned combat damage first.&quot;). A player assigning damage to these two Caitlyns and one unit with no abilities could choose to fulfill both Caitlyns&#x27; Tank requirements by assigning them both damage before the other unit.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">460.2.c.9.</div><div class="rule-text">If a unit cannot be dealt damage, then no amount of damage can be considered lethal. Such a unit is exempt from any considerations of mandatory assignment. Example: Kayn, Unleashed says &quot;If I have moved twice this turn, I don&#x27;t take damage.&quot; While Kayn can&#x27;t take damage, it is ignored for the purposes of assigning lethal damage in combat.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">460.2.d.</div><div class="rule-text">Deal Damage to each unit equal to the amount assigned to it.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">460.3.</div><div class="rule-text">2. Skip the FEPR process and proceed to the Resolution Step.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">461.</div><div class="rule-text">Step 3: The Resolution Step</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">461.1.</div><div class="rule-text">1. Perform a Combat Cleanup.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">461.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Invoke a Combat Special Cleanup.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-3"><div class="rule-id">461.1.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Insert &quot;3c. Heal all Units. &quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">461.1.a.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Insert &quot;3d. Recall Attackers present at the Battlefield if Defenders are still present.&quot; See rule 449. Recalls for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">461.2.</div><div class="rule-text">The following Task becomes Outstanding:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">461.3.</div><div class="rule-text">1. Determine Combat Result</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">461.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">A Player has won a combat if they received either the attacker or defender designation and are the only Player that has units remaining at this battlefield during this step.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">461.3.b.</div><div class="rule-text">A Player has lost a combat if they received either the attacker or defender designation and are the only Player that does not have any units remaining at this battlefield during this step.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">461.3.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Units at this battlefield inherit the same combat result as their controllers</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">461.3.d.</div><div class="rule-text">There is &quot;No Result&quot; if either both Players have units present during this step, or neither player has units present during this step.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">461.3.d.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If &quot;No Result&quot; was reached, and both players have units remaining, stage a Combat at this battlefield.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">461.</div><div class="rule-text">4 The following Task becomes Outstanding:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">461.5.</div><div class="rule-text">1. If no Showdown or Combat is staged at this location, the player with Units remaining here Establishes Control .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">461.5.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Clear the Contested Status .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">461.5.b.</div><div class="rule-text">If there are no Units remaining here controlled by any player, the Battlefield becomes Uncontrolled.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">461.5.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Remove all Hidden cards from this Battlefield that do not share a controller with the Battlefield .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">461.5.d.</div><div class="rule-text">Establishing Control results in a Conquer if that player has not yet scored this Battlefield this turn. See rule 185. Control for more information on Control. See rule 464.1. for more information on Conquering.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">461.5.e.</div><div class="rule-text">This does not have to be the player that applied Contested to the Battlefield.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">461.6.</div><div class="rule-text">The following Task becomes Outstanding :</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">461.7.</div><div class="rule-text">1. Combat ends.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">461.7.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Remove Attacker and Defender Designation from all Units and Players .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">461.7.</div><div class="rule-text">b All &quot;this combat&quot; effects expire simultaneously.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">462.</div><div class="rule-text">Scoring</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">463.</div><div class="rule-text">Scoring is the act of a Player gaining a point through the process of seizing or maintaining control over Battlefields .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">463.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Every instance of Scoring is also an instance of Gaining points</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">464.</div><div class="rule-text">A player Scores in one of two ways:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">464.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Conquer: A player gains Control of a Battlefield they did not yet Score this turn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">464.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">In Modes of Play with teammates, Battlefields under the Control of a teammate during the Beginning Phase are also disqualified from being Scored through Conquer by any means.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">464.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">A player will gain control of a Battlefield after establishing Control by applying Contested first.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">464.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Hold: A player maintains Control of a Battlefield during their Beginning Phase.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">465.</div><div class="rule-text">A player may only Score , from either method, once per Battlefield per turn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">466.</div><div class="rule-text">When a player Scores , two things occur:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">466.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The player Gains up to one Point , depending on their current score.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">466.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The Winning Point has additional restrictions.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">466.1.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Notably, points Gained from sources that are not Conquer or Hold are not beholden to these restrictions.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">466.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">When a player tries to Gain a Point through a Score , and their current Point Total is 1 point from the Victory Score of the Mode of Play or higher, the following occurs:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">466.1.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If the player has Scored through Hold , that player Gains the Winning Point.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">466.1.b.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If the player has Scored through a Conquer and has Scored every Battlefield through either method this turn, that player Gains the Winning Point. If the player has Scored through a Conquer and has not Scored every Battlefield this turn, that player draws a card.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">466.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Trigger Score abilities at the Battlefield that Scored.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">466.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Conquer abilities trigger at a Battlefield that was Conquered.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">466.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Hold abilities trigger at a Battlefield that was Held.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">466.2.c.</div><div class="rule-text">These will only trigger when the Battlefield is Scored; I.E. These cannot be triggered more than once per turn for a player.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">467.</div><div class="rule-text">When a cleanup occurs and a player has accrued Points greater than or equal to the Victory Score for their Mode of Play, and if they have more points than any opponent, they Win the Game .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">468.</div><div class="rule-text">Layers</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">469.</div><div class="rule-text">Layers are the mechanism in which Game Effects alter the Traits, Intrinsic Abilities, or other properties of Game Objects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">470.</div><div class="rule-text">Layers are an organizational structure.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">470.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Layers only serve to structure the application and order that Game Effects apply to Game Objects to maintain consistency.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">471.</div><div class="rule-text">The layers are applied repeatedly until all effects operating on objects have been applied once and no changes have been processed.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">471.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Layers are applied in sequence. Each effect in them is applied as soon as able, and only a single time across all sequences.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">471.2.</div><div class="rule-text">When a sequence of applications completes, recur the process, and evaluate each layer again applying any effects that may now be applicable.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">471.3.</div><div class="rule-text">The removal or disqualification of an effect is separate from the application of the effect, but still can only be applied once. Example: Fiora, Victorious has printed Might 4 and says &quot;While I&#x27;m Mighty, I have Deflect, Ganking, and Shield.&quot; If a player places a buff on Fiora, her Might is increased in the Arithmetic layer, after the layer for Ability-Altering Effects. The Ability-Altering Effect layer is then re-checked and the abilities Deflect, Ganking, and Shield applied. Since each effect has been applied once and there are no other effects to apply, Fiora&#x27;s characteristics are finalized as 5 Might with Deflect, Ganking, and Shield. While a buffed Fiora, Victorious is in combat as a defender, an additional +1 Might will be applied in the Arithmetic layer, giving her 6 Might and the 3 keywords. Example: A buffed Fiora, Victorious is in combat as a defender when her buff is removed. Reevaluating the layers in sequence, she no longer gains Deflect, Ganking, and Shield during the Ability-Altering Effect layer, so when the Arithmetic layer is evaluated, neither the buff (which is gone) nor Shield (which she no longer has) apply. She goes directly from 6 Might with three keywords to 4 Might with no keywords.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">472.</div><div class="rule-text">Layers are applied in the following order:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">472.1.</div><div class="rule-text">1. Trait-Altering Effects</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">472.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">This layer deals with effects that grant, remove, or replace inherent traits of Game Objects. Name Super Type Type Tags Controller Cost Domain</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">472.1.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Assignment of Might is dealt with in this layer. Example: A spell reads &quot;A unit&#x27;s Might becomes 4 this turn.&quot; The unit&#x27;s Might is set to 4 in this layer.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">472.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Copy effects are applied in this layer.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">472.1.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">When one Game Object becomes a copy of another, all Traits, including the Rules Text, replace or are added to those of the original Game Object as specified by the Game Effect directing the Copy. This is applied in this layer.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">472.1.b.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Some Game Effects may specify copying certain traits of a card - only the traits specified by the Game Effect will be copied.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">472.1.b.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Copy effects will copy the copyable traits of a Game Object: by default, those are the printed traits of the Game Object . When a Game Object becomes a copy of something, its copyable traits are updated to the new traits it has received. Example: A player triggers Leblanc, Deceiver&#x27;s hold effect and plays a Reflection token, making it a copy of Honest Broker. That player then plays Mirror Image, targeting the Reflection token. When the Mirror Image Reflection token is played, it copies all of the copyable traits of the original Reflection token - which are currently those of Honest Broker which it is a copy of. That player will have three units named Honest Broker in play, two of which are token Copies with Temporary.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">472.1.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Effects for this layer can be identified by the phrase &quot;become(s)&quot;, &quot;give,&quot; &quot;is,&quot; or &quot;are&quot; in the text. Example: A permanent has the ability &quot;Other friendly units are Yordles.&quot; Other friendly units gain the Yordle tag in this layer.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">472.2.</div><div class="rule-text">2. Ability-Altering Effects</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">472.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">This layer deals with effects that grant, remove, or replace the abilities or rules text of Game Objects . Keywords Passive Abilities Appending rules text Removing rules text Duplicating Rules Text from one Game Object to another</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">472.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Effects for this layer can be identified by the phrase &quot;become(s),&quot; &quot;give,&quot; &quot;lose(s),&quot; &quot;have,&quot; &quot;has,&quot; &quot;is,&quot; or &quot;are&quot; in the text. Example: A permanent has the ability &quot;Other friendly units have [Vision].&quot; Other friendly units gain the Vision keyword in this layer.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">472.2.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Abilities of Effect Text of Attached cards are appended in this layer.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">472.3.</div><div class="rule-text">3. Arithmetic</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">472.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">This layer deals with the mathematics of increasing and decreasing the numeric values of the traits of Game Objects. Might Energy Cost Power Cost</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">472.3.b.</div><div class="rule-text">When an arithmetic effect has a limitation that applies, it is limited at the time of its application, and is &quot;remembered&quot; at that limited level for the duration of its effect. This process is called &quot;snapshotting.&quot; Example: If an effect gives a unit &quot;-4 [M] to a min of 1 this turn&quot; choosing a unit with 2 [M], then the effect will generate -1 [M] this turn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">472.3.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Might Bonuses of Attached cards are applied in this layer.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">472.3.d.</div><div class="rule-text">This layer applies arithmetic in the following way.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-3"><div class="rule-id">472.3.d.1.</div><div class="rule-text">1. Increases</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-4"><div class="rule-id">472.3.d.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Positive values, or increases, to Might are applied first.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-4"><div class="rule-id">472.3.d.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">If there is a restriction or limitation to this increase, the limitation is &quot;snapshotted&quot; for the duration of the effect.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-3"><div class="rule-id">472.3.d.2.</div><div class="rule-text">2. Decreases</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-4"><div class="rule-id">472.3.d.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Negative values, or decreases, to Might are applied last.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-4"><div class="rule-id">472.3.d.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">If there is a restriction or limitation to this decrease, the limitation is snapshotted for the duration of the effect.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">473.</div><div class="rule-text">If more than one effect applies to the same Game Object in the Same Layer , or to each other in the same layer, then both effects will apply but their order may be determined by Dependency.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">473.1.</div><div class="rule-text">A Dependency is established if:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">473.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Applying one of the effects alters the existence of the other; or</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">473.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Applying one of the effects alters the number of objects the other effect can influence</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">473.1.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Applying one of the effects alters the outcome when applying the other.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">474.</div><div class="rule-text">To determine which effect Depends on another, determine which of the prior criteria applies, and then also which effect&#x27;s evaluation is altered by the sequence of applications. That effect is said to Depend on the other.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">474.1.</div><div class="rule-text">To resolve a dependency, the effects within the same layer that created the dependency must be applied such that: 1. Identify which effect Depends on the other within the Layer. 2. Apply the effect that is depended on first. 3. Immediately apply the effect that Depends on the first effect next.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">475.</div><div class="rule-text">If more than one effect applies in the same layer but no dependency is established, then Timestamp order is applied to the effects within that layer and sublayer</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">475.1.</div><div class="rule-text">When an effect begins applying, it establishes a time for which it is compared against other Game Effects for purposes of resolving Layered effects as its Timestamp.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">475.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Timestamps are not rote values.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">475.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Timestamps are relative comparisons between effects and when they began applying to the game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">475.1.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Timestamps are not referenced by Game Effects in any way. They are only used to finalize layered effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">475.2.</div><div class="rule-text">When Rules Text becomes Inactive for any reason, it loses its Timestamp. When it ceases to be Inactive, a new Timestamp is established.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">475.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Effects are applied such that the earliest Timestamp within each Layer and Sublayer applies first, followed by other Effects in that Layer and Sublayer in chronological order.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">476.</div><div class="rule-text">Modes of Play</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">477.</div><div class="rule-text">There are multiple methods of playing Riftbound.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">478.</div><div class="rule-text">A Mode of Play must define several variables for the game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">478.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Number of Players : How many people are playing the game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">478.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Formation of Players : How the players are organized while playing.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">478.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">This defines if a player is alone or on a team.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">478.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">This defines the number of opponents.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">478.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Victory Score: The point total a player or team must reach to win.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">478.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Victory Scores can be any positive number.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">478.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefield Count: Determines how many Battlefields are in play, contributed by players, during play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">478.4.a.</div><div class="rule-text">This may influence deck building requirements in competitive settings.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">478.4.b.</div><div class="rule-text">This may involve utilizing less Battlefields than there are players.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">478.5.</div><div class="rule-text">Setup: Any changes to initial setup required for this mode.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">478.6.</div><div class="rule-text">Format: Conditions to win or additional rules added over play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">478.7.</div><div class="rule-text">First Turn Process: Adjustments to each player&#x27;s first turn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">478.8.</div><div class="rule-text">Unique Rules</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">478.8.a.</div><div class="rule-text">If any, they will be appended here.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">479.</div><div class="rule-text">Sanctioned Modes</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">480.</div><div class="rule-text">1v1 (Duel)</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">480.1.</div><div class="rule-text">2 Players</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">480.2.</div><div class="rule-text">1v1 1 opponent each No teams</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">480.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Victory Score: 8</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">480.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefield Count: 2</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">480.4.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Each player provides three (3) Battlefields , included in their deck during deck building. Only 1 will be used, chosen during setup.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">480.5.</div><div class="rule-text">Setup: Each player randomly selects one (1) of their three (3) Battlefields . The other two are removed and will not be used for this game. The selected Battlefields are placed simultaneously in the Battlefield Zone.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">480.6.</div><div class="rule-text">Format: Best of 1. The first player to reach the Victory Score in Points wins the Match.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">480.7.</div><div class="rule-text">First Turn Process: The player going second channels an extra Rune from their Rune Deck during their first Channel Phase of the game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">481.</div><div class="rule-text">1v1 (Match)</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">481.1.</div><div class="rule-text">2 Players</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">481.2.</div><div class="rule-text">1v1 1 opponent each No teams</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">481.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Victory Score: 8</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">481.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefield Count: 2</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">481.4.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Each player provides three (3) Battlefields , included in their deck during deck building. Only 1 will be used, chosen during setup.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">481.5.</div><div class="rule-text">Setup: Each player selects one (1) of their three (3) Battlefields . The other two are set aside and will not be used for this round of play. The selected Battlefields are placed simultaneously in the Battlefield Zone . After this game, the Battlefields that were used are to be removed and not selected again for this Match . One of the remaining Battlefields that were set aside must be chosen instead.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">481.6.</div><div class="rule-text">Format: Best of 3. The first player to reach the Victory Score in Points wins the game. The winner of that game earns One Game Win. Players then reset the game state, remove the Battlefields in play from the game, choose new Battlefields from those set aside, and play again. The first player to earn Two Game Wins wins the match.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">481.7.</div><div class="rule-text">First Turn Process: The player going second channels an extra Rune from their Rune Deck during their first Channel Phase of the game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">482.</div><div class="rule-text">FFA3 (Skirmish)</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">482.1.</div><div class="rule-text">3 Players</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">482.2.</div><div class="rule-text">FFA 2 opponents each No teams</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">482.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Victory Score: 8</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">482.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefield Count: 3</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">482.4.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Each player provides three (3) Battlefields, included in their deck during deck building. Only 1 will be used, chosen during setup.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">482.5.</div><div class="rule-text">Setup: Each player randomly selects one (1) of their three (3) Battlefields . The other two are discarded and will not be used for this game. The selected Battlefields are placed simultaneously between the three Players before play and will be used for this game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">482.6.</div><div class="rule-text">Format: Best of 1. The first player to reach the Victory Score in Points wins the Match.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">482.7.</div><div class="rule-text">First Turn Process: The player going first does not draw a card during their first Draw Phase of the game. The player going last channels an extra Rune from their Rune Deck during their first Channel Phase of the game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">483.</div><div class="rule-text">FFA4 (War)</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">483.1.</div><div class="rule-text">4 Players</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">483.2.</div><div class="rule-text">FFA 3 opponents each No teams</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">483.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Victory Score: 8</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">483.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefield Count: 3</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">483.4.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Each player provides three (3) Battlefields , included in their deck during deck building.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">483.4.b.</div><div class="rule-text">The player who is taking the first turn removes their Battlefields. They will not be used.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">483.5.</div><div class="rule-text">Setup: Each player who is not going first randomly selects one (1) of their three (3) Battlefields . The other two are removed and will not be used for this game. The selected Battlefields are placed simultaneously between the players before play and will be used for this game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">483.6.</div><div class="rule-text">Format: Best of 1. The first player to reach the Victory Score in Points wins the Match.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">483.7.</div><div class="rule-text">First Turn Process: The player going first does not draw a card during their first Draw Phase of the game. The player going last channels an extra Rune from their Rune Deck during their first Channel Phase of the game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">484.</div><div class="rule-text">2v2 (Magma Chamber)</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">484.1.</div><div class="rule-text">4 Players</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">484.2.</div><div class="rule-text">2v2 2 opponents each 1 teammate</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">484.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Victory Score: 11</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">484.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefield Count: 3</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">484.4.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Each player provides three (3) Battlefields , included in their deck during deck building.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">484.5.</div><div class="rule-text">Setup:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">484.5.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Each player who is not going first randomly selects one (1) of their three (3) Battlefields . The other two are removed and will not be used for this game. The selected Battlefields are placed simultaneously between the players before play and will be used for this game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">484.5.b.</div><div class="rule-text">The player who is taking the first turn removes their Battlefields. They will not be used.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">484.5.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Turn order alternates teams.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">484.5.c.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The first player will be followed by an opponent, then the first player&#x27;s teammate, then the first opponent&#x27;s teammate, and so on.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">484.5.c.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If allies are sitting across from each other, turn order proceeds clockwise as normal.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">484.5.c.3.</div><div class="rule-text">If allies are sitting next to each other, turn order is passed across the table.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">484.6.</div><div class="rule-text">Format: Best of 1. The first team to reach the Victory Score in Points wins the Match.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">484.6.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Teammates win or lose together.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">484.6.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If one player Concedes , then the entire team loses.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">484.6.a.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If one player Loses, then the entire team loses.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">484.6.a.3.</div><div class="rule-text">If one player Wins , then the entire team wins.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">484.7.</div><div class="rule-text">First Turn Process: The player going first does not draw a card during their first Draw Phase of the game. The player going last channels an extra Rune from their Rune Deck during their first Channel Phase of the game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">484.8.</div><div class="rule-text">Unique Rules</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">484.8.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Players may play spells or activate abilities during their Teammate&#x27;s Turn. In order to do so, their Teammate will invite them to play a spell or activate an ability using their own Priority.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">484.8.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields controlled during the Beginning Phase of a player&#x27;s turn by that player&#x27;s teammate are disqualified from being scored by that Team, that turn. Example: A player may not induce their partner to retreat, and then conquer a Battlefield their teammate was controlling.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">484.8.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Control is not shared.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">484.8.c.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Players may not Hide cards at Battlefields controlled by their Teammate.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">484.8.c.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Players may not issue Standard Movement to their Teammate&#x27;s Units.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">484.8.d.</div><div class="rule-text">Friendly describes controlled Game Objects by a player or their Teammate. Example: &quot;When I am played, ready a friendly unit &quot; could target a player&#x27;s own Units or their teammate&#x27;s Units.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">484.8.e.</div><div class="rule-text">Hands are Private Information. Players may show their Private Information to one or more players at any time during play, including their teammate.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">484.8.e.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Revealing Cards is still a game action and cannot be done unless instructed. See rule 424. Reveal for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">484.8.f.</div><div class="rule-text">The Final Point has an adjustment to the criteria when scoring.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">484.8.f.1.</div><div class="rule-text">When scoring the Final Point from Conquer , a player must Score each Battlefield in the same turn, excepting any that were occupied by their ally during that turn&#x27;s Beginning Phase .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">484.8.f.2.</div><div class="rule-text">No other changes to Final Point restrictions.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">484.8.g.</div><div class="rule-text">Teammates may not utilize the same Champion Legend.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">484.8.h.</div><div class="rule-text">Teammates may not utilize the same Battlefields.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">649.</div><div class="rule-text">Conceding</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">650.</div><div class="rule-text">A player may concede at any time.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">651.</div><div class="rule-text">When a player concedes, they are removed from the game in progress.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">651.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If only one other player is remaining after a player has conceded, the player remaining Wins.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">651.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If more than one player remains after a concession, follow the steps for the Removal of a Player.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">651.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Removal of a player involves them no longer being able to make choices or otherwise influence the game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">651.4.</div><div class="rule-text">If the player has Teammates due to the Mode of Play , that player&#x27;s Teammates also lose and are removed from the game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">652.</div><div class="rule-text">If the game continues, follow these steps for Removal of a Player.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">652.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Banish all permanents, runes, and facedown cards they currently control and all permanents, runes, and facedown cards they own.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">652.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Remove the Battlefield they contributed to the game if it is in use.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">652.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">If it was in use, Replace it with a token battlefield with no abilities.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">652.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Any units or hidden cards there do not move and are otherwise unaffected by this process. See rule 438. Replace for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">652.2.c.</div><div class="rule-text">If the removed battlefield was applying any continuous effects, those continuous effects immediately cease, which may cause changes in the characteristics of units or hidden cards there. Example: A battlefield reads &quot;Units here have +1 [M].&quot; If that battlefield&#x27;s owner concedes and the battlefield is removed from the game as a result, units there immediately cease to get +1 [M].</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">652.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Remove all cards they own from the game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">652.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Counter all spells and abilities of all types controlled by the player that has conceded.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">652.5.</div><div class="rule-text">Proceed with the game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">652.5.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Turn</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">652.5.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If the removed player was the Turn Player , play proceeds in Turn Order to the next available player in order.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">652.5.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Focus</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">652.5.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If the removed player had Focus in a Showdown , the next Player in order receives Focus .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">652.5.b.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If the player being removed creates a state where all Players have Passed their Focus , the Showdown ends and play proceeds as necessary, E.G. Combat is resolved or a Cleanup is completed.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">652.5.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Priority</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">652.5.c.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If the removed player had Priority during a Chain , the next Player in order receives Priority .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">652.5.c.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If the player being removed creates a state where all Players have passed Priority , then the most recent spell or ability on the Chain will resolve with Priority being re-established as appropriate for the state after the resolution of that spell or ability.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-chapter level-0"><div class="rule-id">700.</div><div class="rule-text">Additional Rules</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">701.</div><div class="rule-text">Buffs</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">702.</div><div class="rule-text">Buffs are objects placed on Units.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">702.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Buffs can be tracked with a buff reminder card from a Riftbound booster pack or with any spare object in your surroundings.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">702.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Buffs can be added or spent.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">702.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">To Buff a Unit , a player chooses a Unit and then places a buff on it. That Unit is Buffed for as long as the buff remains on it.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">702.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Spending a Buff removes a single Buff counter from a Unit .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">702.2.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">A buff cannot be spent from a Unit that does not have a buff.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">702.2.b.2.</div><div class="rule-text">A player can only spend buffs on units they control.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">702.3.</div><div class="rule-text">There can only be one Buff on a Unit at a time.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">702.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">If a Buff is added, or instructed to be added, on a Unit that already has a Buff , it is not placed instead.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">703.</div><div class="rule-text">Each Buff individually contributes +1 Might to a Unit.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">704.</div><div class="rule-text">Buffs are Game Objects and may be referenced, counted, or targeted by other effects as specified.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">705.</div><div class="rule-text">If a Unit leaves play, remove all Buffs from it.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">705.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Champions do not retain Buffs in the Champion Zone, even if they return there somehow.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">706.</div><div class="rule-text">Mighty</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">707.</div><div class="rule-text">Mighty is a description that applies to some units. Other game effects can check whether a unit is Mighty.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">708.</div><div class="rule-text">A Unit &quot;is Mighty&quot; as long as its Might is 5 or greater.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">709.</div><div class="rule-text">A Unit &quot;becomes Mighty&quot; at the moment its Might changes from being less than 5 to being 5 or greater. Example: A Unit with Might 4 that gets +1 [M] becomes Mighty . Example: A Unit with Might 5 that gets +1 [M] does not become Mighty , because it was already Mighty.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">710.</div><div class="rule-text">Units on the board are evaluated according to their current Might. Example: A unit with a base Might of 3 is targeted by a spell that reads &quot;A unit gets +3 [M] this turn.&quot; As that spell resolves, its Might changes from 3 to 6, and it becomes Mighty . When that effect expires at the end of the turn, it will no longer be Mighty.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">711.</div><div class="rule-text">Units in Non-Board Zones are evaluated according to their inherent Might. Example: A unit in the trash is Mighty if its printed Might is 5 or greater. It doesn&#x27;t matter if there were effects raising or lowering its might while it was on the board.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">712.</div><div class="rule-text">Bonus Damage</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">713.</div><div class="rule-text">Bonus Damage is an intrinsic property that can be granted to Deal actions that influence the amount of Damage that the action is distributing.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">714.</div><div class="rule-text">If more than one instance of Bonus Damage is applied or granted to a Deal action, all instances are summed and applied once.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">714.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Bonus Damage can only be a positive value, and can only increase the amount of Damage being distributed.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">714.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If, for any reason, Bonus Damage would be a negative number, then no Bonus Damage is applied to the action.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">715.</div><div class="rule-text">Bonus Damage applies to the total damage Dealt by one instance of the action.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">715.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If the Deal action has a single target, the amount of Damage to that target will be increased by the Bonus Damage granted to it.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">715.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If the Deal action has multiple targets, the amount of Damage dealt to each target is increased by Bonus Damage individually and separately. Example: Singularity is a spell that says &quot;Deal 6 to each of up to two units.&quot; A player plays Singularity while they also control Annie, Fiery, a unit that says &quot;Your spells and abilities deal 1 Bonus Damage.&quot; Singularity deals 1 Bonus Damage to both of its targets, dealing 7 to each.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">715.3.</div><div class="rule-text">If the Deal action Splits damage, then the Bonus Damage applies to the amount of Damage that will be Split . This can alter the number of targets eligible to be chosen. Example: Volibear, Furious is a unit that says in part &quot;When I attack, deal 5 damage split among any number of enemy units here.&quot; A player attacks with Volibear, Furious while they also control Annie, Fiery, a unit that says &quot;Your spells and abilities deal 1 Bonus Damage.&quot; Volibear, Furious now deals 6 damage split among any number of enemy units at its location, and can choose to split that damage among up to 6 units rather than the usual 5.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">715.4.</div><div class="rule-text">If no damage was Dealt, because it was replaced or reduced by any means, then Bonus Damage will not apply.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">716.</div><div class="rule-text">Attachment</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">717.</div><div class="rule-text">Attaching is a limited action that causes cards to become linked to each other to combine their effects in some way.
